（104年度入學新生適用）

104.04.22一○三學年度第五次教務會議通過

106.11.15 一○六學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Students are required to take one two-credit course in each category. This is a eight-credit course.</p><p>此二學分學生可自由選擇，由通識講座課程、微課自主學習或通識四大領域課程中選課。惟按所屬院（系）之不同，學生選修四大領域課程時需符合以下規定：</p><p>This is a two-credit course. Students are free to choose:<br/>The General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit and Self-Study course or Four Distributive Studies categories.</p><p>Four Distributive Studies categories must have the following requirements:</p><table><tr><td><p>(系)院</p><p>(Dept.)College</p></td><td><p>選課規定</p><p>Course requirements</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>工學院</p><p>College of Engineering</p></td><td><p>不得再選自然領域(GN)，須於社會(GS),生命(LS),人文藝術(LE)三領域中選課</p><p>General Education courses in the area of Nature Science are not required; please select the courses among the areas of GS, LS and LE.</p></td></tr></table></td></tr><tr><td><p>人格特質（6）</p></td><td><p>問題創意思解</p><p>IE232</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td><p>研究方法</p><p>IE233</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td><p>工程溝通<br/>IE231</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="4"><p>系</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>（67）</p></td><td><p>微積分(一)</p><p>IE109</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>微積分(二)</p><p>IE110</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>工程統計</p><p>IE203</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>工程統計（二）</p><p>IE204</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>作業研究</p><p>IE303</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>作業研究（二）</p><p>IE329</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>畢業專題<br/>IE440</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>工業工程實務專題<br/>IE426</p><p>(1)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>工業工程概論</p><p>IE101</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>工程圖學</p><p>IE114</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>製造程序</p><p>IE209</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>網路資訊應用<br/>IE212<br/>(3)</p></td><td><p>生產計劃與管制（一）</p><p>IE335</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>生產計劃與管制 (含實驗) （二）<br/>IE348</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>資訊概論</p><p>IE117</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>計算機程式</p><p>IE215</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>資料庫管理系統IE406<br/>(3)</p></td><td><p>工業會計</p><p>IE301</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>品質管制<br/>(含實驗)<br/>IE350</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>設施規劃<br/>(含實驗)<br/>IE349</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>資訊概論實務</p><p>IE118</p><p>(1)</p></td><td><p>線性代數（含演習）</p><p>IE217</p><p>(4)</p></td><td><p>人因工程(一)</p><p>IE220</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td><p>工程經濟<br/>IE308</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分</p><p>小計</p></td><td><p>11</p></td><td><p>13</p></td><td><p>12</p></td><td><p>11</p></td><td><p>12</p></td><td><p>11</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>1</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>** 最低畢業學分 – 必修：106學分；選修：22學分。</p><p>1.	一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。</p><p>2.	「工業工程實務專題」須於大四下學期修習，但成績優異符合提前畢業者可另案申請。</p><p>3.	擋修科目(須達及格60分)：微積分(一) →微積分(二)、    微積分(二)→工程統計、</p><p>工程統計→工程統計(二)、     工程統計→品質管制</p><p>4.	擋修科目若不及格，必須連續重修(不准隔年重修)；違反規定者，不給成績。</p><p>5.	外系相關科目至多可承認9學分為系選修，但選讀輔系或本系參與之跨系學程者，至多可承認12學分。	</p><p>6.	獲准五年一貫的學生在大學部修習研究所課程之學分，若計入大學畢業學分數內，不得於研究所採認。</p><p>7. 有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>8. 畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。</p><p>9.【IE440畢業專題】為終端學習課。</p></td></tr></table>

Graduation Project IE440(2) can be counted toward department electives.</p><ol><li>凡修畢本系規定學程之課程者，將由本系授與各學程證書。</li></ol><p>IEM will issue Program completion certificate upon completing IEM required study program.</p></td></tr></table>

# **人因工程與設計學程**

（105年度入學新生適用）

105.04.20  一○四學年第五次教務會議通過

# **學程介紹**

「人因工程與設計學程」的主要宗旨除了培養學生俱備人因工程的專業知識外，並訓練學生將人因工程應用於各種設計（如工具、儀器設備、電子產品、車輛、網頁、應用軟體、醫療器材、電動遊戲、工作環境及服務等）。透過本學程所安排的課程教學、專業實習、甚至研究，學生將能以「人」為出發點與任何設計人員共同設計、開發出同時俱備設計感與高可用性的產品。

# **課程規劃**

## 必修課程：4門選3門 ( 9學分)  + <u>人因工程與設計專題（2學分）</u>

<table><tr><td><p>課號</p></td><td><p>課程名稱</p></td><td><p>必/選修</p></td><td><p>學分</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE121</p></td><td><p>工業設計</p></td><td><p>選修</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE220</p></td><td><p>人因工程（一）</p></td><td><p>必修</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE243</p><p>AD115</p></td><td><p>產品設計思維</p><p>設計創作(一)</p></td><td><p>選修</p><p>系必修</p></td><td><p>3</p><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE313</p></td><td><p>人因工程（二）</p></td><td><p>選修</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>人因工程與設計專題*</p></td><td></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr></table>

<u>\*「人因工程與設計專題」可以各系之「畢業專題」相關課程抵免，但專題內容須與人因工程與設計有關。</u>

## 選修課程：_<strong><u>8</u></strong><u>門選3門（9學分）</u>

<table><tr><td><p>課號</p></td><td><p>課程名稱</p></td><td><p>學分</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE237</p></td><td><p>統計建模與電腦化實作</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE304</p></td><td><p>應用統計分析</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE245</p></td><td><p>服務工程</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE351</p></td><td><p>3D互動數位內容製作</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE356</p><p>IC190</p></td><td><p>行動應用程式設計與開發</p><p>行動裝置程式設計 </p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IC294 </p></td><td><p>穿戴式科技設計（一）</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ME388/AD313</p></td><td><p>藝術與設計創作（一）</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ME339/AD314</p></td><td><p>藝術與設計創作（二）</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr></table>

註：必修課程<u>5</u>門全選者，選修課程可選 <u>2</u>門。

學程證書授與標準：凡修畢十一學分的必修課程及至少三門選修課程，共二十學分，經學程負責單位審查無誤後，由工學院授與「人因工程與設計學程」學程證明書。

**學程證書授與標準：** 凡修畢本學程必修課程、及至少四門的選修課程，共十五學分，經學程負責單位審查無誤後，由工學院授與「工業 4.0－智慧生產」學程證明書。

graduation requirement: complete both 106 credits for required courses and 22 credits for elective courses.</p><p>1.	一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。Introduction to Intelligent Production IE101 must be completed within the 1st year enrolled in IEM major, which includes both freshman &amp; transferred student.</p><p>2.	「工業工程實務專題」須於大四下學期修習，但成績優異符合提前畢業者可另案申請。Practical **元智大學工業工程與管理學系 學程修業規定**

**（106學年度入學新生適用for Admission in Academic Year 2017: Fall 2017 & Spring 2018）**

# 106.04.26 一○五學年第五次教務會議通過

# Passed by the 5<sup>th</sup> Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017 on April 26, 2017

本系規劃之學程課程<strong><u>限定在本系選修</u>，</strong>不開放外系課程抵免。若一門課同時有二個學程以上，只能擇一學程計算（資訊類課程除外）。

IEM Program courses must be completed as listed. No substitution courses from outside of IEM department will be allowed. If the course is available in more than one Programs, it can only be counted once (except information/computer related courses).

- 服務科學與資訊學程Service Science & Information Technology Program：

資訊類課程：10門選2門-6學分

Information Technology courses: Select 2 out of 10, total 6 credits

# **人因工程與設計學程**

**（106學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2017. Sept.\~）**

# 106.04.26 一○五學年第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017 on April 26, 2017

106.06.22 一○五學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017, on June 22, 2017

# **課程規劃Study Plan**

# 必修課程：4門選3門 ( 9學分)  + <u>人因工程與設計專題（2學分</u>

# Required：Select 3 out of 4 +<u>_Human Factors and Design Project</u>, total 11 credits

<table><tr><td><p>課號course code</p></td><td><p>課程名稱course name</p></td><td><p>必/選修</p><p>require/                              elective</p></td><td><p>學分credits</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE121</p></td><td><p>工業設計</p><p>Introduction to Industrial Design</p></td><td><p>選修</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE220</p></td><td><p>人因工程（一）</p><p>Human Factors(I)</p></td><td><p>必修</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE243</p><p>AD115</p></td><td><p>產品設計思維</p><p>Product Design</p><p>設計創作</p><p>Design Studio(I)</p></td><td><p>選修</p><p>系必修</p></td><td><p>3</p><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE313</p></td><td><p>人因工程（二）</p><p>Human Factors(II)</p></td><td><p>選修</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>人因工程與設計專題*</p></td><td></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr></table>

<u>\*「人因工程與設計專題」可以各系之「畢業專題」相關課程抵免，但專題內容須與人因工程與設計有關。</u>

\*<u>「Human Factors and Design Project」can be substituted by the Graduation Project of your own department, but it must be related to Human Factors.</u>

## 選修課程：<u>_9門選3門（9學分）</u>

## Elective：Select 3 out of 8, total 9 credits

<table><tr><td><p>課號</p></td><td><p>課程名稱</p></td><td><p>學分</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE237</p></td><td><p>統計建模與電腦化實作</p><p>Statistical Modeling and Computerized Implementations</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE304</p></td><td><p>應用統計分析</p><p>Applied Statistical Analysis</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE245</p></td><td><p>服務工程</p><p>Service Engineering</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE351</p></td><td><p>3D互動數位內容製作</p><p>Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE356</p></td><td><p>行動應用程式設計與開發</p><p>Design and Development of Mobile Application</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>EE479</p></td><td><p>人機互動概論</p><p>Human-Computer Interaction</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ME388/AD313</p></td><td><p>藝術與設計創作（一）</p><p>Art &amp; Design Studio(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>AD314</p></td><td><p>藝術與設計創作（二）</p><p>Art &amp; Design Studio(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>EE492</p></td><td><p>工程應用生理學</p><p>Bioengineering Physiology</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr></table>

註：必修課程<u>5</u>門全選者，選修課程可選 <u>2</u>門。

Note: If complete all 5 courses from the required category, thus only need to complete 2 elective courses.

學程證書授與標準：凡修畢十一學分的必修課程及至少三門選修課程，共二十學分，經學程負責單位審查無誤後，由工學院授與「人因工程與設計學程」學程證明書。

Program Certificate standard of issue: must complete 11 credits of required courses and at least 3 elective courses (total of 20 credits); once approved by the authorized department, College of Engineering will issue 「Human factors and design program」Program Certificate.

**Industrial Engineering and Management at Yuan Ze University**

(Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="17"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="17"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="17"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士學位學程、資訊學院英語學士學位學程、人文社會學院英語學士學位學程、電機通訊學院英語學士學位學程學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>人格特質<strong>(6)</strong></p></td><td><p>問題創意思解</p><p>Creative freshman &amp; transferred student.</li><li>「工業工程實務專題」須於大四下學期修習，但成績優異符合提前畢業者可另案申請。Practical Operations of Industrial Engineering IE426 must be taken in the 2nd semester of senior year. However, student with top grade or exceptional performance can apply for early completing.</li><li>擋修科目：prerequisite</li></ol><p>微積分（一）Calculus (I) （須達及格60分） →  微積分（二）Calculus (II)、     </p><p>    微積分（二）Calculus (II) （須達及格60分）  →  工程統計Engineering Statistics、</p><p>工程統計 Engineering Statistics（須達及格50分）→工程統計（二）Engineering Statistics (II)、</p><p>工程統計Engineering Statistics（須達及格60分） → 品質管制(含實驗) Quality Control (Lab)</p><ol><li>擋修科目若不及格，必須連續重修（不准隔年重修）；違反規定者，不給成績。Not satisfying prerequisite, student must re-take the course immediately (skipping is not allowed); grades will not be issued for any one not following the regulation.</li><li>獲准五年一貫的學生在大學部修習研究所課程之學分，若計入大學畢業學分數內，不得於研究所採認。Any graduate level courses taken during the undergrad and counted toward undergrad graduation requirement, which cannot be counted into the 5-year Master’s Program.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>  通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>  The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>「IE440畢業專題」為終端學習課。IE440 Graduation Project serves as the terminal learning course.</li><li>課程「IE220人因工程（一）」及「IE232問題創意思解」為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」 Course code IE220,Course code IE232 are compulsory courses of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses"</li><li>課程資料庫管理系統 (課號IE406))、網路資訊應用 (課號IE212)、3D互動數位內容製作(課號IE351)、多媒體應用(課號IE427)、虛擬實境系統設計與建構 (課號IE619)、資料視覺課程(課號IE574)、巨量資料分析 (課號IE625) 、物聯網概論與實務(課號IE626)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須修習通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。Database Management Systems (IE406), Network Information Application (IE212), Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content (IE351) , Multimedia Application (IE427) ,Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems(course code IE625) , Data Visualization(course code IE574), Big Data Analytics(IE625) ,Introduction and Practice of Internet of Things (IoT)( IE626) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require taking passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</li><li>本系同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修70學分，選修27學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。Student of Dept. of Ad must take 000 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (00), and Department Elective courses (00). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</li><li>畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and related cross departmental program.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

本系規劃之學程課程<strong><u>限定在本系選修</u>，</strong>不開放外系課程抵免。若一門課同時有二個學程以上，只能擇一學程計算（資訊類課程除外）。

IEM Program courses must be completed as listed. No substitution courses from outside of IEM department will be allowed. If the course is available in more than one Programs, it can only be counted once (except information/computer related courses).

學程證書授與標準：

凡修畢學程課程十五學分(至少含必修課程六學分)與人因工程與設計相關專題兩學分，經學程負責單位審查無誤後，由工學院授與「人因工程與設計學程」學程證明書。

Program Certificate standard of issue: must compelete 15 credits of the program courses (with at least 6 credits of required courses) and 2 credits of Human Factors and Design related project; once approved by the authorized department, College of Engineering will issue the “Human Factors and Design Program” program certificate.

# **電子化供應鏈學程**

# **E-Supply Chain Management Program**

# **107學年度入學新生適用**

# **for Admission in Academic Year 2018: Fall 2018 & Spring 2019**

107.06.27 一○六學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017, on June 27, 2018

# **課程規劃Study Plan**

必修課程：共11學分

Required : Total 11 credits

<table><tr><td><p><strong>課號</strong>course code</p></td><td><p><strong>課程名稱</strong>course name</p></td><td><p><strong>開課學系</strong>Department </p></td><td><p><strong>學分數</strong>credits</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE120</p></td><td><p>RFID概論</p><p>Introduction to RFID</p></td><td><p>工管IEM</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE312</p><p>IM424</p><p>CM302</p></td><td><p>物流管理</p><p>Logistics Management</p><p>供應鏈管理導論</p><p>Introduction to Supply Chain Management</p><p>供應鏈管理</p><p>Supply Chain Management</p></td><td><p>工管IEM</p><p>資管IM</p><p>管院CM</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>IE352</p><p>CM350</p></td><td><p>國際物流管理</p><p>Internationl Logistics Management</p><p>全球運籌管理</p><p>Global Logistics Management</p></td><td><p>工管IEM</p><p>管院CM</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>全球運籌實務專題*</p></td><td><p>各系</p></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr></table>

\* 可以各系至少兩學分之「畢業專題」相關課程抵免，但專題內容須與全球運籌管理、供應鏈管理、物流等議題相關。

\* can be substituted by the Graduation Project of your own department, but it must be related to Global Logistics Management, Supply Chain Management, Logistics Management, etc.

**選修課程：至少選兩門課程，共6學分**

**Elective : At least 2 courses, 6 credits**

**學程證書授與標準：**

凡修畢十一學分的必修課程、及至少兩門的選修課程，共十七學分，經學程負責單位審查無誤後，由工學院授與「電子化供應鏈」學程證明書。

Program Certificate standard of issue: must complete 11 credits of required courses and at least 2 elective courses (total of 17 credits); once approved by the authorized department, College of Engineering will issue “E-Supply Chain Management Program”Program Certificate.

freshman &amp; transferred student.</li><li>「工業工程實務專題」須於大四下學期修習，但成績優異符合提前畢業者可另案申請。Practical Operations of Industrial Engineering IE426 must be taken in the 2nd semester of senior year. However, student with top grade or exceptional performance can apply for early completing.</li><li>擋修科目：prerequisite</li></ol><p>微積分（一）Calculus (I) （須達及格60分） →  微積分（二）Calculus (II)、     </p><p>    微積分（二）Calculus (II) （須達及格60分）  →  工程統計Engineering Statistics、</p><p>工程統計 Engineering Statistics （須達及格50分）→工程統計（二）Engineering Statistics (II)、</p><p>   工程統計Engineering Statistics（須達及格60分） → 品質管制(含實驗) Quality Control (Lab)</p><ol><li>擋修科目若不及格，必須連續重修（不准隔年重修）；違反規定者，不給成績。Not satisfying prerequisite, student must re-take the course immediately (skipping is not allowed); grades will not be issued for any one not following the regulation.</li><li>獲准五年一貫的學生在大學部修習研究所課程之學分，若計入大學畢業學分數內，不得於研究所採認。Any graduate level courses taken during the undergrad and counted toward undergrad graduation requirement, which cannot be counted into the 5-year Master’s Program.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>  通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>  The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>「IE440畢業專題」為終端學習課。IE440 Graduation Project serves as the terminal learning course.</li><li>課程「IE220人因工程（一）」及「IE232問題創意思解」為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」 Course code IE220,Course code IE232 are compulsory courses of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses"</li><li>課程資料庫管理系統(課號IE406)、網路資訊應用(課號IE212)、3D互動數位內容製作(課號IE351)、多媒體應用(課號IE427)、虛擬實境系統設計與建構 (課號IE619)、資料視覺(課號IE574)、巨量資料分析(一) (課號IE628)、巨量資料分析(二) (課號IE629)、物聯網概論與實務(課號IE626)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須修習通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。Database Management Systems (IE406), Network Information Application (IE212), Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content (IE351) , Multimedia Application (IE427) ,Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems(IE625) , Data Visualization(IE574), Big Data Analytics(I)(IE628) , Big Data Analytics(II)(IE629), Introduction and Practice of Internet of Things (IoT)( IE626) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require taking passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</li><li>本系同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修70學分，選修27學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。Student of Dept. of Ad must take 128 credits in total for graduation ,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (70), and Department Elective courses (27). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</li><li>畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and related cross departmental program.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系 學程修業規定**

**108學年度入學新生適用**

**for Admission in Academic Year 2020: Fall 2020 & Spring 2021**

108.05.01 一○七學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2018, on May 01, 2019

108.11.13 一○八學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on November 13, 2019

本系規劃之學程課程<strong><u>限定在本系選修</u>，</strong>不開放外系課程抵免。若一門課同時有二個學程以上，只能擇一學程計算（資訊類課程除外）。

IEM Program courses must be completed as listed. No substitution courses from outside of IEM department will be allowed. If the course is available in more than one Programs, it can only be counted once (except information/computer related courses).

- 服務科學與資訊學程Service Science & Information Technology Program：

資訊類課程：11門選2門-6學分

Information Technology courses: Select 2 out of 10, total 6 credits

學程證書授與標準：凡取得以上資訊類課程2門及服務類課程3門之學分者，授與「服務與資訊學程」證書。Program Certificate requirement: 2 courses of Information & 3 courses of Service programs will issue certificate of “Service Science & Information Technology Program”.

- 品質與資訊學程Quality Management & Information Technology Program：

**Industrial Engineering and Management at Yuan Ze University**

Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="17"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="17"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>人格特質<strong>(6)</strong></p></td><td><p>問題創意思解</p><p>Creative 最低畢業學分：必修：102學分；選修：26學分。</p><p>** Minimum graduation requirement: complete both 102 credits for required courses and 26 credits for elective courses.</p><ol><li>一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。Introduction to Intelligent Production IE101 must be completed within the 1st year enrolled in IEM major, which includes both freshman &amp; transferred student.</li><li>「工業工程實務專題」須於大四下學期修習，但成績優異符合提前畢業者可另案申請。Practical Operations of Industrial Engineering IE426 must be taken in the 2nd semester of senior year. However, student with top grade or exceptional performance can apply for early completing.</li><li>擋修科目：prerequisite</li></ol><p>微積分（一）Calculus (I) （須達及格60分） →  微積分（二）Calculus (II)、     </p><p>    微積分（二）Calculus (II) （須達及格60分）  →  工程統計Engineering Statistics、</p><p>工程統計 Engineering Statistics （須達及格50分）→工程統計（二）Engineering Statistics (II)、</p><p>   工程統計Engineering Statistics（須達及格60分） → 品質管制(含實驗) Quality Control (Lab)</p><ol><li>擋修科目若不及格，必須連續重修（不准隔年重修）；違反規定者，不給成績。Not satisfying prerequisite, student must re-take the course immediately (skipping is not allowed); grades will not be issued for any one not following the regulation.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>  通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>  The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>「IE439畢業專題」為終端學習課程。IE439 Graduation Project serves as the terminal learning course.</li><li>「IE220人因工程（一）」及「IE232問題創意思解」為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」 Course code IE220,Course code IE232 are compulsory courses of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses"</li><li>課程資料庫管理系統(課號IE406)、網路資訊應用(課號IE212)、3D互動數位內容製作(課號IE351)、多媒體應用(課號IE427)、虛擬實境系統設計與建構 (課號IE619)、資料視覺(課號IE574)、巨量資料分析(一) (課號IE628)、巨量資料分析(二) (課號IE629)、物聯網概論與實務(課號IE626)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須修習通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。Database Management Systems (IE406), Network Information Application (IE212), Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content (IE351) , Multimedia Application (IE427) ,Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems(IE625) , Data Visualization(IE574), Big Data Analytics(I)(IE628) , Big Data Analytics(II)(IE629), Introduction and Practice of Internet of Things (IoT)( IE626) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require taking passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</li><li>本系同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修71學分，選修26學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。Student of Dept. of Ad must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (71), and Department Elective courses (26). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</li><li>畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。凡修畢前述學程，將由本系授與各學程證書。</li></ol><p>IEM will issue Program completion certificate upon completing IEM required program.</p><p>Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and Interdisciplinary Course Program.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系 學程修業規定**

**109學年度入學新生適用**

**for Admission in Academic Year 2020: Fall 2020 & Spring 2021**

109.11.11 一○九學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on November 11, 2020

本系規劃之學程課程<strong><u>限定在本系選修</u>，</strong>不開放外系課程抵免。若一門課同時有二個學程以上，只能擇一學程計算（資訊類課程除外）。IEM Program courses must be completed as listed. No substitution courses from outside of IEM department will be allowed. If the course is available in more than one Programs, it can only be counted once (except information/computer related courses).

- 服務科學與資訊學程Service Science & Information Technology Program：

資訊類課程：11門選2門-6學分

凡修畢學程課程十五學分(至少含必修課程六學分)，經學程負責單位審查無誤後，由工學院授與「人因工程與設計學程」學程證明書。

Program Certificate standard of issue: must compelete 15 credits of the program courses (with at least 6 credits of required courses); once approved by the authorized department, College of Engineering will issue the “Human Factors and Design Program” program certificate.

Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. 最低畢業學分：必修：102學分；選修：26學分。</p><p>** Minimum graduation requirement: complete both 102 credits for required courses and 26 credits for elective courses.</p><ol><li>一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。Introduction to Intelligent Production IE101 must be completed within the 1st year enrolled in IEM major, which includes both freshman &amp; transferred student.</li><li>「工業工程實務專題」須於大四下學期修習，但成績優異符合提前畢業者可另案申請。Practical Operations of Industrial Engineering IE426 must be taken in the 2nd semester of senior year. However, student with top grade or exceptional performance can apply for early completing.</li><li>擋修科目：prerequisite</li></ol><p>微積分（一）Calculus (I) （須達及格60分） →  微積分（二）Calculus (II)、     </p><p>    微積分（二）Calculus (II) （須達及格60分）  →  工程統計Engineering Statistics、</p><p>工程統計 Engineering Statistics （須達及格50分）→工程統計（二）Engineering Statistics (II)、</p><p>    工程統計Engineering Statistics（須達及格60分） → 品質管制(含實驗) Quality Control (Lab)</p><ol><li>擋修科目若不及格，必須連續重修（不准隔年重修）；違反規定者，不給成績。Not satisfying prerequisite, student must re-take the course immediately (skipping is not allowed); grades will not be issued for any one not following the regulation.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>  通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>  The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>「IE439畢業專題」為終端學習課。IE439 Graduation Project serves as the terminal learning course.</li><li>「IE220人因工程（一）」及「IE232問題創意思解」為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」</li></ol><p> Course code IE220,Course code IE232 are compulsory courses of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses"</p><ol><li>畢業前須修習通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」，可至本系或外系修習。本系「數位應用相關課程｣ 包含基礎物聯網應用與實作(IE122)、網路資訊應用(IE212)、系統模擬與應用(IE247)、3D互動數位內容製作(IE351)、資料庫管理系統(IE406)、多媒體應用(IE427)、深度學習神經網路概論與實作(IE438)、資料視覺(IE574)、虛擬實境系統設計與建構 (IE619)、物聯網概論與實務(IE626)、巨量資料分析(一) (IE628)及巨量資料分析(二) (IE629)等課程。</li></ol><p>Students require taking passing at least two 'digital application courses'. Fundamental Applications and Practices of Internet of Things(IE122), Network Information Application (IE212), System Simulation and Applications(IE247), Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content (IE351), Database Management Systems (IE406), Multimedia Application (IE427), Introduction and Practices to Deep Learning Neural Networks(IE438), Data Visualization(IE574), Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems(IE625), Introduction and Practice of Internet of Things (IoT)( IE626), Big Data Analytics(I)(IE628), Big Data Analytics(II)(IE629) are courses of 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修71學分，選修26學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (71), and Department Elective courses (26). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p><ol><li>畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。凡修畢前述學程，將由本系授與各學程證書。</li></ol><p>IEM will issue Program completion certificate upon completing IEM required program.</p><p>Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and Interdisciplinary Course Program.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系 學程修業規定**

**110學年度入學新生適用**

**for Admission in Academic Year 2021: Fall 2021 & Spring 2022**

109.11.11 一○九學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on November 11, 2020

本系規劃之學程課程<strong><u>限定在本系選修</u>，</strong>不開放外系課程抵免。若一門課同時有二個學程以上，只能擇一學程計算（資訊類課程除外）。IEM Program courses must be completed as listed. No substitution courses from outside of IEM department will be allowed. If the course is available in more than one Programs, it can only be counted once (except information/computer related courses).

- 服務科學與資訊學程Service Science & Information Technology Program：

資訊類課程：11門選2門-6學分

Information Technology courses: Select 2 out of 10, total 6 credits

**學程證書授與標準：** 凡修畢本學程必修課程一門、及至少四門的選修課程，共十五學分，經學程負責單位審查無誤後，由工學院授與「工業 4.0－智慧生產」學程證明書。Program Certificate standard of issue: must complete program required courses and at least 4 elective courses (total of 15 credits); once approved by the authorized department, College of Engineering will issue”Industry 4.0－Intelligent Production” Program Certificate.

(II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td complete both 102 credits for required courses and 26 credits for elective courses.</p><ol><li>一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。Introduction to Intelligent Production IE101 must be completed within the 1st year enrolled in IEM major, which includes both freshman &amp; transferred student.</li><li>大四學生因參與國際交流計畫或因特殊情況，經系主任審核後，可提前修習或免修「工業工程實務專題」，惟仍須符合畢業學分要求方可畢業。Senior students Fundamental Applications and Practices of Internet of Things(IE122), Network Information Application (IE212), System Simulation and Applications(IE247), Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content (IE351), Database Management Systems (IE406), Multimedia Application (IE427), Introduction and Practices to Deep Learning Neural Networks(IE438), Data Visualization(IE574), Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems(IE625), Introduction and Practice of Internet of Things (IoT)( IE626), Big Data Analytics(I)(IE628), Big Data Analytics(II)(IE629) are courses of 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修、通識課程、及院必修共31學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (71), and Department Elective courses (26). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p><ol><li>畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。凡修畢前述學程，將由本系授與各學程證書。</li></ol><p>IEM will issue Program completion certificate upon completing IEM required program.</p><p>Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and Interdisciplinary Course Program.</p></td></tr></table>

graduation requirement: complete both 106 credits for required courses and 22 credits for elective courses.</p><p>1.	一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。Introduction to Intelligent However, student with top grade or exceptional performance can apply for early completing.</p><p>3.	擋修科目（須達及格60分）：    微積分（一）Calculus (I)  →  微積分（二）Calculus (II)、     </p><p>   prerequisite (must score 60/100)    微積分（二）Calculus (II)  →  工程統計Engineering Statistics、</p><p>　　　　　　　　　　　　　      工程統計 Engineering Statistics  → 工程統計（二）Engineering Statistics (II)、</p><p>                                工程統計Engineering Statistics  → 品質管制(含實驗) Quality Control (Lab)</p><p>4.	擋修科目若不及格，必須連續重修（不准隔年重修）；違反規定者，不給成績。Not satisfying prerequisite, student must re-take the course immediately (skipping is not allowed); grades will not be issued for any one not following the regulation.</p><p>5.	外系相關科目至多可承認<strong>15</strong>學分為系選修。At the most related <strong>15</strong> credits will be accepted from outside of IEM. </p><p>6.	獲准五年一貫的學生在大學部修習研究所課程之學分，若計入大學畢業學分數內，不得於研究所採認。Any graduate level courses taken during the undergrad and counted toward undergrad graduation requirement, which cannot be counted into the 5-year Master’s Program.</p><p>7. 有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。Must follow the 「Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations」for all related rules on University Compulsory and General Education.</p><p>8. 通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>9. 畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and related cross departmental program.</p><p>  10.「IE440畢業專題」為終端學習課。IE440 Graduation Project serves as the terminal learning course. </p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系 學程修業規定**

**（106學年度入學新生適用for Admission in Academic Year 2017: Fall 2017 & Spring 2018）**

# 106.04.26 一○五學年第五次教務會議通過

# Passed by the 5<sup>th</sup> Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017 on April 26, 2017

本系規劃之學程課程<strong><u>限定在本系選修</u>，</strong>不開放外系課程抵免。若一門課同時有二個學程以上，只能擇一學程計算（資訊類課程除外）。

IEM Program courses must be completed as listed. No substitution courses from outside of IEM department will be allowed. If the course is available in more than one Programs, it can only be counted once (except information/computer related courses).

- 服務科學與資訊學程Service Science & Information Technology Program：

資訊類課程：10門選2門-6學分

Information Technology courses: Select 2 out of 10, total 6 credits

- 製造與資訊學程Production Management & Information Technology Program：

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p>英語檢定English Testing （2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td></td><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td courses.</p><ol><li>一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。Introduction to Intelligent Production IE101 must be completed within the 1st year enrolled in IEM major, which includes both freshman &amp; transferred student.</li><li>大四學生因參與國際交流計畫或因特殊情況，經系主任審核後，可提前修習或免修「工業工程實務專題」，惟仍須符合畢業學分要求方可畢業。Senior students participating in international exchange programs or facing special circumstances may, upon approval of the department head, take in advance or be exempted from the IE426 "Practical Operations of Industrial Engineering" course. Fundamental Applications and Practices of Internet of Things(IE122), Network Information Application (IE212), System Simulation and Applications(IE247), Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content (IE351), Database Management Systems (IE406), Multimedia Application (IE427), Introduction and Practices to Deep Learning Neural Networks(IE438) are courses of 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分，（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses（27）credits , College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming（4）credits. (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit.)</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><ol><li>畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。凡修畢前述學程，將由本系授與各學程證書。</li></ol><p>IEM will issue Program completion certificate upon completing IEM required program.</p><p>Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and Interdisciplinary Course Program.</p></td></tr></table>

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2025)**

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><p>2.	English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</p><p>3.	English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </p><p>4.	Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><p>5.	“English Testing” (EL160) is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>6.	<strong>Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. </strong>The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</p><p>7. The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' (EL375).</p><p> 英語檢定English Testing（2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1） </p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td></td><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td credits for required courses and 27credits for elective courses.</p><ol><li>一年級之「工業工程概論」為基礎課程，除轉學生補修之同學需在入學第一年內修得此學分，其他同學必需在一年級內修完。Introduction to Intelligent Production IE101 must be completed within the 1st year enrolled in IEM major, which includes both freshman &amp; transferred student.</li><li>擋修科目：prerequisite</li></ol><p>    工程統計 Engineering Statistics （須達50分）→工程統計（二）Engineering Statistics courses"</p><ol><li>畢業前須修習通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」，可至本系或外系修習。本系「數位應用相關課程｣ 包含基礎物聯網應用與實作(IE122)、網路資訊應用(IE212)、系統模擬與應用(IE247)、3D互動數位內容製作(IE351)、資料庫管理系統(IE406)、多媒體應用(IE427)、深度學習神經網路概論與實作(IE438)等課程。</li></ol><p>Students require taking passing at least two 'digital application courses'. Fundamental Applications and Practices of Internet of Things(IE122), Network Information Application (IE212), System Simulation and Applications(IE247), Implementation of 3D Interactive Digital Content (IE351), Database Management Systems (IE406), Multimedia Application (IE427), Introduction and Practices to Deep Learning Neural Networks(IE438) are courses of 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>大四學生因參與國際交流計畫或因特殊情況，經系主任審核後，可提前修習或免修「工業工程實務專題」，惟仍須符合畢業學分要求方可畢業。Senior students participating in international exchange programs or facing special circumstances may, upon approval of the department head, take in advance or be exempted from the IE426 "Practical Operations of Industrial Engineering" course. However, students still need to meet the graduation credit requirements for graduation.</li><li><a></a>本系同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、本系必修70學分，選修27學分（自由選修至多承認17學分，<strong>含專業自主學習2學分。</strong>與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。（建議寫法：只須符合規定，依據各系選修學分表示方式即可）</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take128credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses（27）credits , College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming（4）credits , Department Compulsory courses（70）credits, and Department Elective courses（27）credits.（A maximum of （17） credits can be recognized for free electives, including（2）credits for Disciplinary Self-Directed Learning. For the cooperation courses with other departments, credits will be recognized according to the specific program regulations.）</p><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><ol><li>畢業前需完成一個學程，包含本系學程、本系參與之跨院系學程。凡修畢前述學程，將由本系授與各學程證書。</li></ol><p>IEM will issue Program completion certificate upon completing IEM required program.</p><p>Must complete a program prior graduation, including IEM program and Interdisciplinary Course Program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF09 (1.3 版)／104.01.06 修訂

註：

1. 必修科目18學分及選修科目3學分。

18 credits of required courses and 3 credits of elective courses are required for the minor.

2. 必修科目在主系已修習該課程者，申請以選修科目取代。

If a required course has been taken in his/her major, the student may replace it with an elective course.

3. 選修科目在主系已修習該課程者，仍應於其他選修科目修滿3學分。

If an elective course has been taken in his/her major, the student still needs to take 3 credits from other elective courses.

4. 修習本系輔系之學生需修滿21 (含) 學分以上者，授與輔系資格。

Students pursuing a minor in this department must complete at least 21 credits (inclusive) to be awarded the minor qualification.
```

**元智大學　工業工程與管理研究所碩士班**

**必修科目表**

**（105學年度入學新生適用）**

105.04.20 一○四學年第五次教務會議通過

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>學期</p><p>科目</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="3"><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(5)</p></td><td><p>書報討論</p><p>(Seminar)</p><p>IE586</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>研究方法論</p><p>(Research Methodology)</p><p>IE999</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學</p><p>分小計</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="4"><p><strong>最低畢業學分：</strong></p><p><strong>必修5學分＋選修24學分＋碩士論文6學分，共計35學分</strong></p><p>須修畢上學期2學分的書報討論、下學期3學分的研究方法論、及8門選修課24學分。在四類中選擇一類作為主修類且至少選修二門課，餘三類至少各選修1門課，共5門課；其餘3門課可自由選修，非本系選修之課程，需先經指導教授及所長同意。</p><p>※非工業工程或工業管理相關學系畢業之碩士班學生，必須選擇下列其中一方案進行課程補修：</p><p>A、選修大學部【生產計劃與管理】課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：【IE531高等品質管制】、【IE538實驗設計】或【IE520田口式品質工程】。</p><p>B、選修大學部【品質管制】課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：【IE534生產排程】、【IE593高等生產管制】或【IE543生產計劃】。</p><p><strong>碩士論文提案 (Proposal) 考試：</strong></p><p>碩士班研究生須於第二學期開學後一個月內決定論文指導教授，並於第三學期十月三十一日前申請提出二人（含指導教授）之論文提案審查委員會。委員會成員由所內專任助理教授級以上組成，針對論文提案進行審查口試。</p><p><strong>碩士學位資格：</strong></p><p>完成碩士論文，並依規定完成論文口試，但需與論文提案口試，至少需相隔二個月。</p><p><strong>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</strong></p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學　工業工程與管理研究所碩士班**

**必修科目表**

**（109學年度入學新生適用）**

109.05.06 一○八學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 06, 2020

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>學期</p><p>科目</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="3"><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(5)</p></td><td><p>書報討論</p><p>(Seminar)</p><p>IE586</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>研究方法論</p><p>(Research Methodology)</p><p>IE999</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學</p><p>分小計</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="4"><p><strong>最低畢業學分：</strong></p><p><strong>必修5學分＋選修24學分＋碩士論文6學分，共計35學分</strong></p><p>須修畢上學期2學分的書報討論、下學期3學分的研究方法論、及8門選修課24學分。在四類中選擇一類作為主修類且至少選修二門課，餘三類至少各選修1門課，共5門課；其餘3門課可自由選修，非本系選修之課程，需先經指導教授及所長同意。</p><p>※非工業工程或工業管理相關學系畢業之碩士班學生，必須選擇下列其中一方案進行課程補修：</p><p>A、選修大學部【生產計劃與管理】課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：【IE531高等品質管制】、【IE538實驗設計】或【IE520田口式品質工程】。</p><p>B、選修大學部【品質管制】課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：【IE534生產排程】、【IE593高等生產管制】或【IE543生產計劃】。</p><p><strong>碩士論文提案 (Proposal) 考試：</strong></p><p>碩士班研究生須於第二學期開學後一個月內決定論文指導教授，並於第三學期十月三十一日前申請提出二人（含指導教授）之論文提案審查委員會。委員會成員由所內專任助理教授級以上組成，針對論文提案進行審查口試。</p><p><strong>碩士學位資格：</strong></p><p>完成碩士論文，並依規定完成論文口試，但需與論文提案口試，至少需相隔二個月。</p><p><strong>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</strong></p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學　工業工程與管理研究所碩士班**

**元智大學　工業工程與管理研究所碩士班**

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系碩士班 必修科目表**

**（111學年度入學新生適用）**

List of Required Courses for Master Program of

Industrial Engineering and Management at Yuan Ze University

（Applicable to Students Admitted for Academic year of 2022-2023）

111.04.20 一一○學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on April 20, 2022

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Amended by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年學期</p><p>科目</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必修</p><p>科目</p><p>(5)</p></td><td><p>書報討論</p><p>(Seminar)</p><p>IE586</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>研究方法論</p><p>(Research Methodology)</p><p>IE999</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="4"><ul><li><strong>最低畢業學分：</strong></li></ul><p><strong>必修5學分＋選修24學分＋碩士論文6學分，共計35學分</strong></p><p>須修畢上學期2學分的書報討論、下學期3學分的研究方法論、及8門選修課24學分。在四類中選擇一類作為主修類且至少選修二門課，餘三類至少各選修1門課，共5門課；其餘3門課可自由選修，非本系選修之課程，需先經指導教授及所長同意。</p><p>※非工業工程或工業管理相關學系畢業之碩士班學生，必須選擇下列其中一方案進行課程補修：</p><p>A、選修大學部【生產計劃與管理】課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：【IE531高等品質管制】、【IE538實驗設計】或【IE520田口式品質工程】。</p><p>B、選修大學部【品質管制】課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：【IE534生產排程】、【IE593高等生產管制】或【IE543生產計劃】。</p><p>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</p><ul><li><strong>碩士論文提案 (Proposal) 考試：</strong></li></ul><p>碩士生需於研究所第一學期開學後一個月內選定指導教授，並繳交指導教授同意書至系辦公室。論文提案審查委員會由本所二人（含指導教授）專任助理教授級以上教師組成，針對論文提案進行審查口試及專業領域相符性檢核，論文提案與畢業論文口試至少需間隔二個月以上。</p><ul><li><strong>碩士學位考試：</strong></li></ul><p>畢業論文口試依校方規定期限內完成「研究生學位考試線上申請」，碩士學位考試委員會置委員三至五人；學生應於學位考試前完成論文原創性比對作業，比對報告標準以不超過20%為原則，並於學位考試當日將「學位論文原創性比對報告書」送交指導教授及學位考試委員參考，進行畢業論文口試及專業領域相符性檢核。完成學位考試後，研究生需再次將最終定稿的論文進行原創性比對作業，並由指導教授確認後，將「學位論文定稿原創性比對檢核表」、「學位論文原創性比對報告書」、及論文送交系辦公室備查。學位考試其他未盡事宜，悉依本校「學則」暨「碩、博士班研究生學位考試細則」辦理。</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系碩士班 必修科目表**

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required Courses for Master Program of**

**Industrial Engineering and Management at Yuan Ze University**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted for the Academic year of 2023-2024）**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議通過

Amended by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on May 31, 2023

<table><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="2"><p>學年(Year)</p><p>學期(Semester)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>必修</p><p>科目</p><p>Required Course</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>書報討論</p><p>(Seminar)</p><p>IE586</p><p>(2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>學分小計</p><p>Total credits</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>備 註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ul><li><strong>修業規定 (Regulations for Course Selection)：</strong></li><li>本所碩士班最低畢業總學分數為32學分，包含2學分必修課、24學分選修課、及6學分碩士論文。</li></ul><p>The minimum total credits required for graduation for the master's program is 32 credits, including 2 credits of a required course, 24 credits of elective courses, and 6 credits of the master's thesis.</p><ul><li>選修課中須於「決策最佳化與全球運籌管理」或「智慧型生產與大數據分析」擇一類作為主修且至少選修4門課(12學分)，另一類為副修至少選修2門課(6學分)，共計6門課(18學分)；其餘6學分可自由選修。</li></ul><p>Among the elective courses, students are required to choose one of the two categories, either " Optimization and Global Logistics Management" or "Intelligent Manufacturing and Big Data Analysis," as their primary focus and take at least 4 courses (12 credits) from that category. The other category will be taken as a secondary focus, and students must take at least 2 courses (6 credits) from it, making a total of 6 courses (18 credits). The remaining 6 credits can be freely chosen from any other courses.</p><ul><li>選修非本系之課程，需先經指導教授及所長同意，且以9學分為上限。</li></ul><p>Students must obtain the consent of their advisor and the department chair before taking elective courses from other departments, with a maximum of 9 credits.</p><ul><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ul><p>Students who wish to take courses across different academic programs must fill out the "Cross-System Courses Application Form" provided by Yuan Ze University. A maximum of 6 credits of such courses may be counted toward graduation.</p><ul><li>外籍生(不含僑生及陸生)得免修「IE586書報討論」，但仍需滿足最低畢業學分數之要求。</li></ul><p>Foreign students (excluding overseas Chinese and students from Mainland China) are exempt from taking the course "IE586 Seminar." However, they still need to fulfill the minimum required credits for graduation.</p><ul><li>大學部非工業工程相關學系之畢業生，須選擇以下A方案或B方案進行課程補修(研究所課程可採計為畢業學分)：</li></ul><p>For undergraduate graduates from non-industrial engineering-related departments, they must choose either Option A or Option B for remedial courses (graduate courses may be counted toward graduation credits):</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備 註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="5"><p>A、選修大學部「IE335生產計劃與管理（一）」課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：「IE531高等品質管制」、「IE533機率分析」或「IE538實驗設計」。</p><p>B、選修大學部「IE350品質管制（含實驗）」課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：「IE534生產排程」、「IE543生產計劃」或「IE593高等生產管制」。</p><p>Option A: one undergraduate course “IE335 Production Planning and Control I” and one from the following graduate courses: “IE531 Advanced Quality Control,” “IE533 Probabilistic Analysis,” or “IE538 Experimental Design.”</p><p>Option B: one undergraduate course “IE350 Quality Control (including experiments)” and one from the following graduate courses: “IE534 Production Scheduling,” “IE543 Production Planning,” or “IE593 Advanced Production Control.”</p><ul><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li></ul><p>All graduate students shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, according to the Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Guideline. Students not passing the Academic Research Ethics Education Course cannot apply for their academic degree exam.</p><ul><li><strong>碩士論文提案考試 (Thesis Proposal Examination )： </strong></li></ul><p>碩士生需於研究所第一學期開學後一個月內選定指導教授，並繳交指導教授同意書至系辦公室。論文提案審查委員會由本所二人（含指導教授）專任助理教授級以上教師組成，針對論文提案進行審查口試及專業領域相符性檢核，論文提案與畢業論文口試至少需間隔二個月以上。</p><p>Master students are required to select an advisor and submit an advisor agreement form to the department office within one month after the start of their first semester. The thesis proposal review committee, composed of two full-time assistant professors or above (including the advisor), will review and examine the thesis proposal and its relevance to the Industrial Engineering and Management professional field. The thesis proposal examination and master degree examination must be held at least two months apart.</p><ul><li><strong>碩士學位考試 (Master Degree Examination)：</strong></li></ul><p>畢業論文口試依校方規定期限內完成「研究生學位考試線上申請」，碩士學位考試委員會置委員三至五人；學生應於學位考試前完成論文原創性比對作業，比對報告標準以不超過20%為原則，並於學位考試當日將「學位論文原創性比對報告書」送交指導教授及學位考試委員參考，進行畢業論文口試及專業領域相符性檢核。完成學位考試後，研究生需再次將最終定稿的論文進行原創性比對作業，並由指導教授確認後，將「學位論文定稿原創性比對檢核表」、「學位論文原創性比對報告書」、及論文送交系辦公室備查。學位考試其他未盡事宜，悉依本校「學則」暨「碩、博士班研究生學位考試細則」辦理。</p><p>The master degree examination must be completed within the deadline specified by the university by submitting an online application for the examination. The master's degree examination committee consists of three to five members. Before the degree examination, the student should complete the originality check for the thesis, and the standard for the comparison report is not to exceed 20%. On the day of the degree examination, the student should submit the "Originality Check Report of the Thesis" to the advisor and the degree examination committee for reference, and undergo the thesis defense and professional field compatibility check. After completing the degree examination, the student should conduct an originality check on the final version of the thesis again. After the advisor confirms it, the "Originality Check Form for Thesis Final Draft," "Originality Check Report of the Thesis," and the thesis should be submitted to the department office for record. Any other matters related to the degree examination shall be handled in accordance with the university's "Academic Regulations" and "Graduate Degree Examination Regulations for Master's and Doctoral Programs."</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系碩士班 選修科目表**

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**Industrial Engineering and Management at Yuan Ze University**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted for the Academic year of 2023-2024）**

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

113.11.20 一一三學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on November 20, 2024

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系碩士班 必修科目表**

**（113學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required Courses for Master Program of**

**Industrial Engineering and Management at Yuan Ze University**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted for the Academic year of 2024-2025）**

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年(Year)</p><p>學期(Semester)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必修</p><p>科目</p><p>Required Course</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>書報討論</p><p>(Seminar)</p><p>IE586</p><p>(2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學分小計</p><p>Total credits</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備 註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ul><li><strong>修業規定 (Regulations for Course Selection)：</strong></li><li>本所碩士班最低畢業總學分數為32學分，包含2學分必修課、24學分選修課、及6學分碩士論文。</li></ul><p>The minimum total credits required for graduation for the master's program is 32 credits, including 2 credits of a required course, 24 credits of elective courses, and 6 credits of the master's thesis.</p><ul><li>選修課中須於「決策最佳化與全球運籌管理」或「智慧型生產與大數據分析」擇一類作為主修且至少選修4門課(12學分)，另一類為副修至少選修2門課(6學分)，共計6門課(18學分)；其餘6學分可自由選修。</li></ul><p>Among the elective courses, students are required to choose one of the two categories, either " Optimization and Global Logistics Management" or "Intelligent Manufacturing and Big Data Analysis," as their primary focus and take at least 4 courses (12 credits) from that category. The other category will be taken as a secondary focus, and students must take at least 2 courses (6 credits) from it, making a total of 6 courses (18 credits). The remaining 6 credits can be freely chosen from any other courses.</p><ul><li>選修非本系之課程，需先經指導教授及所長同意，且以9學分為上限。</li></ul><p>Students must obtain the consent of their advisor and the department chair before taking elective courses from other departments, with a maximum of 9 credits.</p><ul><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ul><p>Students who wish to take courses across different academic programs must fill out the "Cross-System Courses Application Form" provided by Yuan Ze University. A maximum of 6 credits of such courses may be counted toward graduation.</p><ul><li>外籍生(不含僑生及陸生)得免修「IE586書報討論」，但仍需滿足最低畢業學分數之要求。</li></ul><p>Foreign students (excluding overseas Chinese and students from Mainland China) are exempt from taking the course "IE586 Seminar." However, they still need to fulfill the minimum required credits for graduation.</p><ul><li>大學部非工業工程相關學系之畢業生，須選擇以下A方案或B方案進行課程補修(研究所課程可採計為畢業學分)：</li></ul><p>For undergraduate graduates from non-industrial engineering-related departments, they must choose either Option A or Option B for remedial courses (graduate courses may be counted toward graduation credits):</p></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p>備 註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td><p>A、選修大學部「IE335生產計劃與管理（一）」課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：「IE531高等品質管制」、「IE533機率分析」或「IE538實驗設計」。</p><p>B、選修大學部「IE350品質管制（含實驗）」課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：「IE534生產排程」、「IE543生產計劃」或「IE593高等生產管制」。</p><p>Option A: one undergraduate course “IE335 Production Planning and Control I” and one from the following graduate courses: “IE531 Advanced Quality Control,” “IE533 Probabilistic Analysis,” or “IE538 Experimental Design.”</p><p>Option B: one undergraduate course “IE350 Quality Control (including experiments)” and one from the following graduate courses: “IE534 Production Scheduling,” “IE543 Production Planning,” or “IE593 Advanced Production Control.”</p><ul><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li></ul><p>All graduate students shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, according to the Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Guideline. Students not passing the Academic Research Ethics Education Course cannot apply for their academic degree exam.</p><ul><li><strong>碩士論文提案考試 (Thesis Proposal Examination )： </strong></li></ul><p>碩士生需於研究所第一學期開學後一個月內選定指導教授，並繳交指導教授同意書至系辦公室。論文提案審查委員會由本所二人（含指導教授）專任助理教授級以上教師組成，針對論文提案進行審查口試及專業領域相符性檢核，論文提案與畢業論文口試至少需間隔二個月以上。</p><p>Master students are required to select an advisor and submit an advisor agreement form to the department office within one month after the start of their first semester. The thesis proposal review committee, composed of two full-time assistant professors or above (including the advisor), will review and examine the thesis proposal and its relevance to the Industrial Engineering and Management professional field. The thesis proposal examination and master degree examination must be held at least two months apart.</p><ul><li><strong>碩士學位考試 (Master Degree Examination)：</strong></li></ul><p>畢業論文口試依校方規定期限內完成「研究生學位考試線上申請」，碩士學位考試委員會置委員三至五人；學生應於學位考試前完成論文原創性比對作業，比對報告標準以不超過20%為原則，並於學位考試當日將「學位論文原創性比對報告書」送交指導教授及學位考試委員參考，進行畢業論文口試及專業領域相符性檢核。完成學位考試後，研究生需再次將最終定稿的論文進行原創性比對作業，並由指導教授確認後，將「學位論文定稿原創性比對檢核表」、「學位論文原創性比對報告書」、及論文送交系辦公室備查。學位考試其他未盡事宜，悉依本校「學則」暨「碩、博士班研究生學位考試細則」辦理。</p><p>The master degree examination must be completed within the deadline specified by the university by submitting an online application for the examination. The master's degree examination committee consists of three to five members. Before the degree examination, the student should complete the originality check for the thesis, and the standard for the comparison report is not to exceed 20%. On the day of the degree examination, the student should submit the "Originality Check Report of the Thesis" to the advisor and the degree examination committee for reference, and undergo the thesis defense and professional field compatibility check. After completing the degree examination, the student should conduct an originality check on the final version of the thesis again. After the advisor confirms it, the "Originality Check Form for Thesis Final Draft," "Originality Check Report of the Thesis," and the thesis should be submitted to the department office for record. Any other matters related to the degree examination shall be handled in accordance with the university's "Academic Regulations" and "Graduate Degree Examination Regulations for Master's and Doctoral Programs."</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版) / 113.12.16

**元智大學工業工程與管理學系碩士班 必修科目表**

**（113學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required Courses for Master Program of**

**Industrial Engineering and Management at Yuan Ze University**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted for the Academic year of 2024-2025）**

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年(Year)</p><p>學期(Semester)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必修</p><p>科目</p><p>Required Course</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>書報討論</p><p>(Seminar)</p><p>IE586</p><p>(2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學分小計</p><p>Total credits</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備 註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ul><li><strong>修業規定 (Regulations for Course Selection)：</strong></li><li>本所碩士班最低畢業總學分數為32學分，包含2學分必修課、24學分選修課、及6學分碩士論文。</li></ul><p>The minimum total credits required for graduation for the master's program is 32 credits, including 2 credits of a required course, 24 credits of elective courses, and 6 credits of the master's thesis.</p><ul><li>選修課中須於「決策最佳化與全球運籌管理」或「智慧型生產與大數據分析」擇一類作為主修且至少選修4門課(12學分)，另一類為副修至少選修2門課(6學分)，共計6門課(18學分)；其餘6學分可自由選修。</li></ul><p>Among the elective courses, students are required to choose one of the two categories, either " Optimization and Global Logistics Management" or "Intelligent Manufacturing and Big Data Analysis," as their primary focus and take at least 4 courses (12 credits) from that category. The other category will be taken as a secondary focus, and students must take at least 2 courses (6 credits) from it, making a total of 6 courses (18 credits). The remaining 6 credits can be freely chosen from any other courses.</p><ul><li>選修非本系之課程，需先經指導教授及所長同意，且以9學分為上限。</li></ul><p>Students must obtain the consent of their advisor and the department chair before taking elective courses from other departments, with a maximum of 9 credits.</p><ul><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ul><p>Students who wish to take courses across different academic programs must fill out the "Cross-System Courses Application Form" provided by Yuan Ze University. A maximum of 6 credits of such courses may be counted toward graduation.</p><ul><li>外籍生(不含僑生及陸生)得免修「IE586書報討論」，但仍需滿足最低畢業學分數之要求。</li></ul><p>Foreign students (excluding overseas Chinese and students from Mainland China) are exempt from taking the course "IE586 Seminar." However, they still need to fulfill the minimum required credits for graduation.</p><ul><li>大學部非工業工程相關學系之畢業生，須選擇以下A方案或B方案進行課程補修(研究所課程可採計為畢業學分)：</li></ul><p>For undergraduate graduates from non-industrial engineering-related departments, they must choose either Option A or Option B for remedial courses (graduate courses may be counted toward graduation credits):</p></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p>備 註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td><p>A、選修大學部「IE335生產計劃與管理（一）」課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：「IE531高等品質管制」、「IE533機率分析」或「IE538實驗設計」。</p><p>B、選修大學部「IE350品質管制（含實驗）」課程及下列研究所課程中的任一科：「IE534生產排程」、「IE543生產計劃」或「IE593高等生產管制」。</p><p>Option A: one undergraduate course “IE335 Production Planning and Control I” and one from the following graduate courses: “IE531 Advanced Quality Control,” “IE533 Probabilistic Analysis,” or “IE538 Experimental Design.”</p><p>Option B: one undergraduate course “IE350 Quality Control (including experiments)” and one from the following graduate courses: “IE534 Production Scheduling,” “IE543 Production Planning,” or “IE593 Advanced Production Control.”</p><ul><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li></ul><p>All graduate students shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, according to the Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Guideline. Students not passing the Academic Research Ethics Education Course cannot apply for their academic degree exam.</p><ul><li><strong>碩士論文提案考試 (Thesis Proposal Examination )： </strong></li></ul><p>碩士生需於研究所第一學期開學後一個月內選定指導教授，並繳交指導教授同意書至系辦公室。論文提案審查委員會由本所二人（含指導教授）專任助理教授級以上教師組成，針對論文提案進行審查口試及專業領域相符性檢核，論文提案與畢業論文口試至少需間隔二個月以上。</p><p>Master students are required to select an advisor and submit an advisor agreement form to the department office within one month after the start of their first semester. The thesis proposal review committee, composed of two full-time assistant professors or above (including the advisor), will review and examine the thesis proposal and its relevance to the Industrial Engineering and Management professional field. The thesis proposal examination and master degree examination must be held at least two months apart.</p><ul><li><strong>碩士學位考試 (Master Degree Examination)：</strong></li></ul><p>畢業論文口試依校方規定期限內完成「研究生學位考試線上申請」，碩士學位考試委員會置委員三至五人；學生應於學位考試前完成論文原創性比對作業，比對報告標準以不超過20%為原則，並於學位考試當日將「學位論文原創性比對報告書」送交指導教授及學位考試委員參考，進行畢業論文口試及專業領域相符性檢核。完成學位考試後，研究生需再次將最終定稿的論文進行原創性比對作業，並由指導教授確認後，將「學位論文定稿原創性比對檢核表」、「學位論文原創性比對報告書」、及論文送交系辦公室備查。學位考試其他未盡事宜，悉依本校「學則」暨「碩、博士班研究生學位考試細則」辦理。</p><p>The master degree examination must be completed within the deadline specified by the university by submitting an online application for the examination. The master's degree examination committee consists of three to five members. Before the degree examination, the student should complete the originality check for the thesis, and the standard for the comparison report is not to exceed 20%. On the day of the degree examination, the student should submit the "Originality Check Report of the Thesis" to the advisor and the degree examination committee for reference, and undergo the thesis defense and professional field compatibility check. After completing the degree examination, the student should conduct an originality check on the final version of the thesis again. After the advisor confirms it, the "Originality Check Form for Thesis Final Draft," "Originality Check Report of the Thesis," and the thesis should be submitted to the department office for record. Any other matters related to the degree examination shall be handled in accordance with the university's "Academic Regulations" and "Graduate Degree Examination Regulations for Master's and Doctoral Programs."</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版) / 113.12.16
